That allowed accidental or reasonless consent撤回 attempts without the shared confirmation gate used by other pharmacy-cooperation state transitions. Did not wrap the long fan-out in one `withOrgContext` interactive transaction because that would reintroduce timeout risk and defeat fail-soft behavior; explicit `org_id` filters remain the enforced isolation for this pass. Prod migration apply remains human-gated.
- performance issues found: added `@@index([org_id, target_type, target_id, created_at(sort: Desc)])` for AuditLog timeline operation history and `@@index([org_id, patient_id, created_at(sort: Desc)])` for FirstVisitDocument timeline reads; added `take: 8` to first-visit documents; raised timeline-only source concurrency to 8; overlapped source actor-name resolution with the AuditLog query.
